## Findings & Recommendations
- A+/A win rate 39% vs B/C 38% -> KEEP grading
- D-grade filter: filtered signals would have won 27% -> filter justified (<50%)
- 84% rule (Lesson 6 canonical 2026-07-06: solid B&R stop-out arms one re-entry on the reclaim close, ORIGINAL stop + target): 48 triggers, fired win rate 32%.
- 84% live wiring: armed per-symbol off paper stop-outs in live_scanner (2026-07-05). Requires --paper mode; signal-only runs have no stop-out feedback.
- Best setup: one_candle_rule (41%) | worst: reentry_84_rule (32%)
- C-grade alerts (112, alert-only per SPEC2) would have won 31% - similar to traded grades; alert-only demotion costs little.
